print(new_list[1][4])
days_counts = {}
specific_count = 0
new_list = new_list[1:len(new_list)]
for i in range(1,8):
    for j in new_list:
        if int(j[3]) == i:
            specific_count += int(j[4])
    days_counts[i] = specific_count
print(days_counts)
